***лить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a> (5464)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*liti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">litʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полить.html>поли́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:налить.html>нали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pour, to spill</li>
<li>to shed</li>
<li>to cast, to mould, to found</li></ol>

***литься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:литься.html>ли́ться</a> (5978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:литься.html>ли́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политься.html>поли́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вылиться.html>вы́литься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flow, to pour</li>
<li>to pour on oneself</li>
<li>to spread</li>
<li>to sound</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лиф</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lif</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bodice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čik</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***лихо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хо</a> (5439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>лихо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lixój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">líxo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́ха</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>лих</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> evil, ill, misfortune, trouble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>буди́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́ха</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спи́т</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тихо.html>ти́хо</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne budí <b>líxa</b> poká <b>líxo</b> spit (tíxo)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">don't trouble until trouble troubles you</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́йте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хом</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne pominájte <b>líxom</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">remember me kindly, think kindly of me; don't hold the grudge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">said by a person leaving or about to do something risky</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:почем.html>почём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фунт</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́ха</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">uznátʹ, počóm funt <b>líxa</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to fall on hard times, to plumb the depths of misfortune</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to find out the price of evil per pound</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>An odd number, see the <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chetno_i_licho">Chetno i licho</a> game.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">líxo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dashingly, jauntily</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лиходей.html>лиходе́й</a> (30455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***лихой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>лихой</a> (6825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лихъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lixŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lixъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>лихо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lixój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ли́ше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>evil, hard, sinister</li>
<li>valiant, intrepid, bold, daring</li>
<li>dashing, gallant</li>
<li>nimble</li>
<li>smart</li>
<li>criminal, delinquent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Per Zaliznyak, the comparative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ли́ше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">líše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is rare and awkward.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бравый.html>бра́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">brávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">удало́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udalój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодецкий.html>молоде́цкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">molodeckij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелый.html>сме́лый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smélyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храбрый.html>хра́брый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xrábryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***лихорадить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихорадить.html>лихора́дить</a> (24177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лихорадить.html>лихора́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lixoráditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to fever, to burn with fever</li>
<li>to cause fever</li>
<li>to ague <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to strike with an ague, or with a cold fit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицезревший.html>лицезре́вший</a> (22872)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***лицемерный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицемерный.html>лицеме́рный</a> (24012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицемер.html>лицеме́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">licemér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицемерный.html>лицеме́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">licemérnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лицеме́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)лицеме́рней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hypocritical</li></ol>

***лицо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> (110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lice</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">licó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>ли́ца</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>ли́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face</li>
<li>countenance</li>
<li>front</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person, individual, individuality
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">by sight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пот.html>по́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v póte licá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">by the sweat of the brow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot licá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the name of</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>licóm</b> k</i> ― <span class="e-translation">facing to, facing towards</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">licóm k licú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">face to face</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицу́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>licóm</b> k <b>licú</b> s</i> ― <span class="e-translation">face to face with</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">net <b>licá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">be bewildered</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:физический.html>физи́ческое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">fizíčeskoje licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">natural person</span></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pérvoje licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">first person</span></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лик.html>лик</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чный</a> (414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">licó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">líčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>personal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to a particular person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> personal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чное</a> местоиме́ние</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">líčnoje mestoiménije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">personal pronoun</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lišáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишайник.html>лиша́йник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišájnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишайник.html>лиша́йника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишайник.html>лиша́йники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишайник.html>лиша́йников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lichen (symbiotic organism)</li>
<li>consortium</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a> (7881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lišítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deprive, to rob, to bereave</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to devest, to forjudge, to dispossess
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive / rob (smb.) of his rights</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наследство.html>насле́дства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> naslédstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disinherit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воинский.html>во́инских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звание.html>зва́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> vóinskix zvánij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reduce to the ranks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> slóva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deny (smb.) the right to speak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парламентский.html>парла́ментского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мандат.html>манда́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> parlámentskovo mandáta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unseat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> sebjá udovólʹstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> sebjá žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take one's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:духовный.html>духо́вного</a> са́на</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> duxóvnovo sána</i> ― <span class="e-translation">defrock, unfrock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лоса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> práva gólosa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданский.html>гражда́нских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> graždánskix prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:родительский.html>роди́тельских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišátʹ</b> rodítelʹskix prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive of parental rights</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
